Guidance on handling user data removal requests When a user asks to erase their account, it’s not enough to just disable login—they must be assured their data is completely unrecoverable. This means purging not just the primary database but also audit trails, cached copies, and third-party integrations. I’ve seen too many firms get fined for assuming deletion equals deactivation. Please audit your retention policies and respond with a clear timeline.
